I've lost count how many times I've ordered directly (I don't use food delivery services) from Blue Line Pizza in Daly City. I haven't tried everything on the menu, but I do highly recommend the Classic Sliders, Pulled Pork Sliders, Chicken Caesar Salad, and Deep Dish Cheese pizza. Customer service is always friendly & accommodating. However, I have to give a special shout out to my fav Benjamin. When taking my phone order he's always personable, thorough, and fast without making you feel rushed. I highly recommend Blue Line Pizza!< /Review>

< review>
Came here after work on Friday to unwind and was greeted warmly by our friendly bartender, Phillip. Service is great - we sat at the bar to eat because it was busy, and he was attentive despite having to run around and serve many people. Even accommodated our requests for extra toppings and gave us solid recommendations for pizza.

My friend, Natalie M., and I split a half bbq chicken/wild mushroom and truffle thin crust pizza that hit the spot just right. Only reason I knocked off a star was the wild mushroom pizza needed some pizzazz and we had to ask for extra jalape√±os and honey to experiment (highly recommend the changes we made) and the bartender needs some work on his cocktail repertoire, but he was open to learning.
All in all...I'm coming back next Friday :) got a new regular, Blue Line.<//review>

< review>
Get the DEEP DISH pizzas here. I got the Indio usual Classic deep dish and it was so yummy -- stuffed with Italian sausage and tomato chunks. But next time I would opt for the actually regular size deep dish pizzas instead. I feel like you get the full deep dish pie experience of a deep dish with all the layers and heaviness of the toppings with the regular sizes. I loved the cornmeal crust -- so delicious.

We also got the personal individual pesto chicken pizza and it tasted healthy and light. It was a bit bland and I would have liked a bit more garlic pesto taste.

Their crust is super on point though! Their salads are good too. I tired the Bacon and Blue salad -- bacon was a bit dry, but I did like the creaminess of the blue cheese and the deep flavors of the grilled onions.

Love their simple menu of pizzas. And especially love that they offer everything in the personal individual size as well. Service was friendly and amazing. Lots of table instead. Super clean and tall floor to ceiling windows. Great place to satisfy your pizza cravings.< /review>

< Text>
I wanted to really write a thorough review on this business regarding my recent visit.

First, I‚Äôd like to say that this isn‚Äôt the first time my dog has been groomed at salcido‚Äôs. My mother took care of my dog for a period of time while I was away in school, so she chose where to get my dog groomed. Up until a little under a year ago, I‚Äôve had my dog with me all of the time and she has a particular groomer and grooming service that I love in the Bay Area of California. However, I‚Äôm staying in the area for a few weeks and my dog needed to be groomed.

Onto my experience, I took my dog in at 10 AM on the dot day of appt. One issue is the fact that I did not receive word of my dog until 2:15 PM. It took almost four and a half hours to finish grooming my dog. The business should allocate time properly and be done with grooming in a timely manner. I am used to 2 hours more or less and 4+ hours is excessive given that my dog did not have any issues with her fur and is a calm and easy-going dog. She also had irritated eyes as they were and still are after several hours, extremely red and her demeanor was down and different than how she usually is.

Second, due to Covid there is a sign saying no one will be serviced or allowed into the building without proper ppe such as a mask. Yet, I physically saw a woman get out of her car without a mask, go into the building without a mask and she was able to retrieve her dog and was not turned away. This is not only not following regulations that are being enforced in California right now, but it also puts at risk other customers, employees and the animals being groomed.

Third, I‚Äôve been to a lot of grooming businesses due to owning multiple poodles, Maltese mixes, and other furry fur babies and at salcido‚Äôs all you hear are dogs crying non-stop. It‚Äôs normal for dogs to whine as they are uncomfortable at times being groomed, but this was excessive and made me worry for my dog‚Äôs well being and safety. To add on to that, I walked in while a dog was crying and the groomer or whoever was attending the dog was speaking roughly to the dog and it did not sound like a good interaction.

Fourth, the employees do not act like or seem to be dog lovers. Usually employees who work with animals are loving and gentle with pets, but these employees are not and that should open the window to how they may treat your pets when you take them. One last thing is that it smells bad inside the business. At drop off, it did not smell like urine and feces, but at pick up it did and it was very strong which does not ease my feelings of how the dogs are waiting to be groomed and where they relieve themselves and if they are relieving out of fear. They also only accept cash, which is a bit inconvenient especially being 2020, but less of a serious issue. I expect the best for my pets and I know a lot of other people do as well so I wanted to share my personal experience and opinion. I will be taking my dog elsewhere.< /Text>

< text>
Found Shear Vanity on Yelp. Made an appointment on Sunday despite the salon being closed on sunday and monday I got a response when I emailed them. I got a call from Esther on the day I wanted to go in and told I'd be good to come in.
I went in for a cut. I went from mid back length hair to just above my shoulders and I love it!!!
Jessica shampooed and conditioned before doing most of the cut and Esther gave it some texture before Jessica finished with the style I had asked for. She knew what to do to get my curly hair to cooperate and it came out great!
The salon is a pretty big size and it's open, clean, and welcoming as was the receptionist at the front.
I felt pampered and I liked the vibe!!
I'm definitely going to go back as I would like to maintain this short length for a while and I'll definitely need to get it trimmed from time to time.
The price is also pretty good, I was expecting a lot more considering I have a lot of hair and I had asked to get it styled as I sat down on the chair instead of mentioning it when I first emailed them.</text>

< text>
I was never a supercuts fan, but here I am writing this review.

Before me coming here, I would go to my local barbershop. Here are a couple of reasons why I switched over.

1. Long waiting line even up to 2hrs to get a haircut, although you called to book an appointment.
2. They only take cash, which is a hassle to waste time at the bank.
3. Some barbers like yapping instead of getting down to business and just cut hair.

Those are a couple of reasons why I come to Supercuts. They get down to business and charge around 20 bucks. At least at this location, when I book an appointment, I don't have to wait to get a haircut, but the most beautiful part of this is they accept debit cards which is a massive advantage for people like myself that hate wasting time at the ATMs.

<gmap_id>0x808f776c94d88b7d:0x130039aa17b8e436</gmap_id>< Text>
After a day of wedding planning we found ourselves quite hungry. As one who craves Korean food all the time. It was only fitting we stumbled across Spicy factory. Even better there was a free large parking lot. No need to parallel park or pay a parking meter. Double Score!

I was not present in line to order, but My Love mentioned they were really friendly! They even gave him a complementary plastic bag to pick up our dog's poop. Also they honored the happy hour snack price for him as well instead of waiting until 3 pm to order again. Not only did they have customer oriented service, but were quick to cook our food. We didn't have to wait very long and was able to devour our meal in no time.

They do have weekday lunch specials that include a few choices of main dishes and two sides. We shared the lunch special "spicy" chicken combo of three wings, two drums, and choice of two sides. Of course we chose both rice and kimchi to accompany our chicken!

Even though the moist chicken isn't as crispy as others expect, it is actually pretty flavorful and has a good amount of heat. The kimchi was fresh and delicious. It was very much appreciated when they securely wrapped the kimchi in foil. The juice didn't find its way everywhere in the to go container. There is also original and honey for those who are interested in more mild flavors.

In addition to the lunch special we had the happy hour snack spicy rice cake. This has been my new favorite Korean food to eat so you can bet I was excited they had it on the menu! In this order it also came with fish cakes, vegetables, melted mozzarella cheese, and red spicy sauce that was just tasty.

I loved how the spicy rice cake snack came out piping hot! It still retained its temperature even after taking pictures and eating it for a bit. Now that I know I like their sauce I will definitely order the larger spicy fried rice cake combo the next go round with the other savory toppings!

Between the two of us we both were satisfied and would say the happy hour and lunch special prices are great deals. Considering the nearby choices I would choose Spicy factory over the other neighboring eats!< /Text>

<pictures>None</pictures><Time>1597822688510</Time>< review>
We just ordered kimchi fries. The portion was huge, but the fries themselves were mediocre. They take frozen shoe string fries (nothing wrong with frozen per se), sprinkle a tiny bit of chopped kimchi on top, and then DROWN it in thousand island sauce (see picture). We thought it was cheese when we first opened the box. We hadn't expected to pay 7 dollars for fries covered in thousand island. We ended up frying up some of our own kimchi and adding it to the fries so that it wouldn't just taste like we were spooning thousand island into our mouths. Fudging up such a simple snack isn't promising, so we probably won't be back.< /review>

<Name>Milo Conway< /Name><rate>4</rate><Resp>None</Resp><userid>114801170749519908100<//userid><GmapID>0x808f776c94d88b7d:0x130039aa17b8e436</GmapID>< time>
1547937401517<//time>
<pics>None< /pics>< text>
Kind of a sparse hole in the wall, much less popular than next door Tiger Tea. However their signature dishes are quite good.

One thing to keep in mind is that their mild is spicy, and it goes up from there.

The rice cake bowl can comfortably feed 2. We did not add any extra toppings as they seem quite pricey. However the dish is quite varied and flavorful as is. One thing I did not like was the hard-boiled eggs which were quite grainy from being overcooked. Otherwise it's simply delectable with a tasty balance of sweet, salty and hot, with all kinds of interesting textures from the rice cakes, gooey mozarella, and crunchy veggies.

The fried chicken were quite large though not the mutant sized you get at Bonchon. Inside was not as moist as the best KFC but still quite acceptable. The crispiness and the flavors are done well, the spicy and the honey are both interesting in their own rights.

Great for a afternoon or late night snack!</text>

Let me first say that the only reason this location is getting 2 stars instead of 1 is because I have been getting my taxes done here for a few years without issue. I wanted to write this review to warn people against using Francis Donahoe as their "tax perfessional". This was my first time dealing with Francis (aka Frank) since my usual person was unavailable. I was slightly frustrated throughout the process because Frank seemed to struggle with the program that they use to file taxes. I thought he was only struggling to read due to font size but near the end I realized he didn't seem to have sufficient knowledge of the program itself. After sitting through a longer than usual tax prep it was time for payment options. I stated that I would pay using my debit card. Frank suggested just having the service fees taken out of my tax refund. I agreed to this and Frank stated he would be sending digital copies of my return to my H&R block account.  Cut to two weeks later and I still haven't received an email confirming that my tax returns had been accepted by the government. < review>
Ranked as one of America, if not world's, clearest and cleanest rivers, the Smith River majestically careens through Northern California's Coastal Mountain Ranges carving gorges and flowing over bedrock until it meets the Pacific Ocean in one of the coasts most active estuaries.  Home to over 13 species of anadromous fish (fish that live in the river and ocean for stages of their life),of which include Chinook and Coho Salmon, Coastal Cutthroat Trout, Steelhead, and Lamprey Eel, to name a few.< /review>

Big thanks to Rainforest Tree Service for the excellent work they performed! We are very happy with the great job you guys did! They arrived early and worked very quickly and methodically to get everything down in the safest way possible. These trees were very close to neighboring houses and fences and the team managed to cut everything and topple it over without so much as breaking a sprinkler!
